TURE).apply {
            putExtra(android.provider.MediaStore.EXTRA_OUTPUT, uri)
        }
    }.getOrNull()

    // ── 广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun registerDownloadReceiver() {
        val filter = IntentFilter(DownloadManager.ACTION_DOWNLOAD_COMPLETE)
        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.TIRAMISU) {
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter, Context.RECEIVER_NOT_EXPORTED)
        } else {
            @Suppress("UnspecifiedRegisterReceiverFlag")
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter)
        }
    }
}
KOTLIN_EOF

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe user says "下载时有系统通知但是下载还是失败了" - there IS a system notification (DownloadManager is being triggered), but the download still fails.\n\nThis means:\n1. The `DownloadManager` path IS being triggered (system notification appears)\n2. But the download itself fails\n\nThis rules out the blob URL issue (which we fixed). The DownloadManager is getting called with an actual URL.\n\nSo the issue must be with the actual DownloadManager request failing. Let me think about why:\n\n**When DownloadManager shows a notification but download fails:**\n\n1. **Authorization header issue**: The `token` prefix might be wrong. GitHub API accepts:\n   - `token <TOKEN>` (classic personal access token)\n   - `Bearer <TOKEN>` (OAuth/fine-grained token)\n   - The existing React code in `downloadWithAuth` uses `Bearer ${token}` but our Android code uses `token $token`\n   - This inconsistency could cause 401 on some token types\n\n2. **Redirect following**: GitHub release assets (`browser_download_url`) typically redirect from `github.com/...` to `objects.githubusercontent.com/...`. DownloadManager follows redirects by default, but the Authorization header might not be forwarded after redirect.\n\n3. **Accept header**: For `browser_download_url`, we set `Accept: application/octet-stream` but GitHub expects different headers.\n\n4. **DownloadManager redirect issue**: When GitHub returns a 302 redirect, DownloadManager might not carry the Authorization header to the redirect URL. For `archive_download_url` (Actions artifacts), GitHub returns a redirect to a pre-signed S3 URL. The Authorization header on the S3 URL would cause a signature mismatch error!\n\nThis is actually a well-known GitHub API issue:\n- For Actions artifacts (`archive_download_url`): GitHub returns 302 → S3 pre-signed URL\n- The S3 URL is already authenticated (pre-signed), so sending Authorization header to S3 would fail with "InvalidAccessKeyId" or similar\n\n5. **DownloadManager SSL/network**: Could be network issues, but less likely since we see the notification.\n\n**Most likely cause: The Authorization header is causing issues with redirected URLs (S3 pre-signed URLs)**\n\nFor GitHub:\n- `archive_download_url` → redirects to AWS S3 pre-signed URL (sending extra auth headers breaks it)\n- `browser_download_url` (release assets) → also redirects\n- `zipball_url` / `tarball_url` → redirect through GitHub\'s CDN\n\nThe React `downloadWithAuth` works because:\n1. `fetch()` follows redirects but sends Authorization to each redirect\n2. Actually `fetch` by default only follows redirects, not necessarily sending the auth header to the redirected URL\n\nWait, actually `fetch` does follow redirects but typically the Authorization header is stripped on cross-origin redirects. Let me think again...\n\nActually, in browsers, for cross-origin redirects, `fetch` with `credentials: \'omit\'` (default for custom headers) will follow the redirect. The Authorization header may or may not be forwarded depending on browser behavior.\n\nFor GitHub API specifically:\n- `archive_download_url`: When you GET with Authorization, GitHub returns 302 to a pre-signed S3 URL. The browser\'s `fetch` follows the redirect but drops the Authorization header (because it\'s a cross-origin redirect to a different domain). The pre-signed S3 URL works without additional auth.\n- DownloadManager: When it gets the 302, it follows the redirect AND forwards the Authorization header, which causes S3 to reject the request (the pre-signed URL doesn\'t expect an Authorization header).\n\n**This is the root cause!**\n\nFor GitHub `archive_download_url` and `browser_download_url`:\n1. First request: GET with Authorization → GitHub returns 302 to S3/CDN URL\n2. DownloadManager follows redirect and sends Authorization to S3 → S3 rejects with 400/403\n\nThe fix: We need DownloadManager to NOT follow redirects blindly with auth headers, OR we need to first resolve the redirect URL manually and then download the final URL without auth.\n\n**Better solution**: Use OkHttp or HttpURLConnection to follow the redirect manually:\n1. GET the GitHub URL with Authorization → get 302 redirect URL\n2. GET the redirect URL WITHOUT Authorization → this is the final S3 pre-signed URL\n3. Pass the final URL to DownloadManager\n\nBut this requires making a network request on Android side, which is complex.\n\n**Alternative simpler fix**: \nSince the React side already has the correct token handling (it works on web), a better approach might be to handle the redirect resolution in a Coroutine or AsyncTask, then give DownloadManager the final URL.\n\nOR, even simpler: Use `HttpURLConnection` with `setFollowRedirects(false)`, get the Location header, then download from the Location URL without auth.\n\nWait, let me reconsider. Let me look at what happens more carefully:\n\nFor `browser_download_url` (GitHub release assets):\n- URL: `https://github.com/user/repo/releases/download/v1.0/file.zip`\n- With Authorization header: GitHub accepts it and may return 302 to `objects.githubusercontent.com/...`\n- DownloadManager follows the redirect and may send the Authorization header again\n- `objects.githubusercontent.com` has its own auth (via query params in the URL already), so extra Authorization header might be rejected\n\nActually, let me reconsider again. Many users successfully use DownloadManager for GitHub downloads. Let me think about what\'s different here.\n\nActually the real issue might be simpler:\n\n**The `Accept: application/octet-stream` header** - this is meant for GitHub API endpoints (like `/repos/{owner}/{repo}/releases/assets/{asset_id}`). But `browser_download_url` is not an API endpoint, it\'s a direct CDN URL. Sending `Accept: application/octet-stream` to it might not matter, but let\'s check if GitHub API version headers cause issues.\n\nActually, the key difference between what works (web fetch) and what fails (DownloadManager):\n\nThe web\'s `downloadWithAuth` uses:\n```javascript\nheaders: {\n    Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,  // Note: Bearer, not token\n    Accept: \'application/vnd.github+json\',\n    \'X-GitHub-Api-Version\': \'2022-11-28\',\n}\n```\n\nOur DownloadManager code uses:\n```kotlin\naddRequestHeader("Authorization", "token $token")  // Note: token, not Bearer\naddRequestHeader("Accept", "application/octet-stream")\n```\n\nTwo differences:\n1. `Bearer` vs `token` prefix - GitHub supports both for PAT tokens, but for fine-grained tokens only `Bearer` works\n2. `Accept` header difference\n\nBut more importantly: the `Accept: \'application/vnd.github+json\'` in the fetch request for a binary file download... that\'s actually wrong too (it asks for JSON but gets binary). But it works because GitHub ignores it for the actual binary response.\n\nActually, looking more carefully at the GitHub API:\n- For `archive_download_url` (Actions artifacts), the correct flow is:\n  1. GET `/repos/{owner}/{repo}/actions/artifacts/{artifact_id}/zip` with Authorization → get 302 to S3 URL\n  2. Download from S3 URL (no extra auth needed)\n\nWhen DownloadManager follows the 302, it will send the Authorization header to the S3 URL, which will cause a `403 SignatureDoesNotMatch` error from S3.\n\n**This is the definitive root cause for artifact downloads.**\n\nFor release asset downloads (`browser_download_url`), the URL is `https://objects.githubusercontent.com/...` which also uses pre-signed URLs after redirect.\n\n**The fix strategy:**\n\n1. **Resolve redirect first, then download the final URL**: \n   - Make an initial HEAD/GET request with auth to the GitHub URL\n   - Follow redirects, capture the final URL\n   - Give DownloadManager the final URL (without auth headers)\n\n2. **Or**: Stream the download manually (using OkHttp) to the Downloads folder, similar to what `saveBlobData` does but streaming instead of loading all in memory.\n\nActually, the cleanest fix for the Android side is to use `HttpURLConnection` or OkHttp to:\n1. Make the initial request with Authorization to get the redirect URL\n2. Then use DownloadManager with the final (no-auth) URL\n\nLet me write this as an Edge Function... wait no. This is pure Android.\n\nLet me write a `resolveRedirectAndDownload` function:\n\n```kotlin\nprivate fun resolveRedirectAndDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {\n    // Run on background thread\n    Thread {\n        runCatching {\n            val connection = java.net.URL(url).openConnection() as java.net.HttpURLConnection\n            connection.apply {\n                setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")\n                setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")\n                instanceFollowRedirects = false  // Don\'t follow automatically\n                requestMethod = "GET"\n                connectTimeout = 15000\n                readTimeout = 15000\n            }\n            connection.connect()\n            val responseCode = connection.responseCode\n            connection.disconnect()\n            \n            when (responseCode) {\n                302, 301, 307, 308 -> {\n                    // Got redirect - use the Location URL directly for DownloadManager\n                    val location = connection.getHeaderField("Location")\n                    if (location != null) {\n                        // Download from the final URL without auth (it\'s pre-signed)\n                        runOnUiThread {\n                            startAuthenticatedDownload(location, fileName, "GitHub Manager Android", "")\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                200 -> {\n                    // No redirect, download directly with auth\n                    runOnUiThread {\n                        startAuthenticatedDownload(url, fileName, "GitHub Manager Android", token)\n                    }\n                }\n                else -> {\n                    runOnUiThread {\n                        Toast.makeText(this, "下载准备失败（${responseCode}）", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }.onFailure { e ->\n            runOnUiThread {\n                // Fallback: try direct download with auth\n                startAuthenticatedDownload(url, fileName, "GitHub Manager Android", token)\n            }\n        }\n    }.start()\n}\n```\n\nBut this approach has an issue: For GitHub archive URLs, the redirect might go through multiple hops. And just following one redirect might not be enough. Also, the redirect URL might expire if we take too long.\n\nA better approach: **Use OkHttp (which is already a dependency in most Android projects via OkHttp) to follow all redirects and get the final URL**.\n\nBut wait, OkHttp isn\'t listed as a dependency in the build.gradle.kts. Let me check what\'s available.\n\nActually, the simplest and most reliable approach is:\n\n**For GitHub artifact/binary downloads**: Don\'t use DownloadManager at all. Instead, use `HttpURLConnection` to stream the download directly to the Downloads folder. This gives us full control.\n\nBut streaming large files is complex. Let me think of a simpler fix.\n\n**Actually, the simplest fix**: Follow redirects manually using `HttpURLConnection` with `instanceFollowRedirects = false`, collect ALL redirect locations, and when we get a non-redirect response, use THAT final URL with DownloadManager (without auth headers - the final URL is pre-signed).\n\n```kotlin\nprivate fun resolveGitHubDownloadUrl(originalUrl: String, token: String): String {\n    var currentUrl = originalUrl\n    var maxRedirects = 5\n    \n    while (maxRedirects-- > 0) {\n        val conn = (java.net.URL(currentUrl).openConnection() as java.net.HttpURLConnection).apply {\n            setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")\n            setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")\n            instanceFollowRedirects = false\n            requestMethod = "HEAD"  // HEAD to avoid downloading body\n            connectTimeout = 10000\n            readTimeout = 10000\n        }\n        conn.connect()\n        val code = conn.responseCode\n        val location = conn.getHeaderField("Location")\n        conn.disconnect()\n        \n        if (code in 300..399 && location != null) {\n            currentUrl = location  // Follow redirect\n        } else {\n            return currentUrl  // This is the final URL\n        }\n    }\n    return currentUrl\n}\n```\n\nBut wait - GitHub\'s 302 for artifact downloads: when you do a HEAD request, does GitHub return 302? Let me think... \n\nFor `archive_download_url` like `/repos/{owner}/{repo}/actions/artifacts/{id}/zip`:\n- The URL requires auth to get the redirect\n- GitHub returns 302 with Location pointing to S3 pre-signed URL\n- The S3 URL can be downloaded directly\n\nFor `browser_download_url` like `https://objects.githubusercontent.com/github-production-release-asset-...`:\n- This is ALREADY the final CDN URL\n- It might not redirect at all\n- With or without auth it might work\n\nHmm, let me reconsider what `browser_download_url` actually looks like. It\'s typically:\n`https://github.com/user/repo/releases/download/v1.0/filename.zip`\n\nWhen accessed:\n1. GitHub checks auth\n2. Redirects to `https://objects.githubusercontent.com/...?response-content-disposition=...&response-content-type=...&...&X-Amz-Signature=...`\n\nThe S3 pre-signed URL has query parameters for auth (X-Amz-Signature etc.). When DownloadManager sends an additional Authorization header to this S3 URL, S3 rejects it because the pre-signed URL already has auth and doesn\'t expect a separate Authorization header.\n\nSo the HEAD + follow redirect approach should work:\n1. HEAD `github.com/releases/download/...` with Authorization → 302 to `objects.githubusercontent.com/...?X-Amz-*=...`\n2. Download from `objects.githubusercontent.com/...?X-Amz-*=...` with DownloadManager (NO auth header)\n\nThis should work! Let me now think about the implementation.\n\nBUT WAIT - GitHub does NOT allow HEAD requests on release download URLs in all cases. Some might return 405. Let me use GET with a small buffer instead... or just follow with GET and disconnect immediately after getting the Location header.\n\nActually, redirects for GitHub release assets work with HEAD requests on the GitHub side. It\'s just a redirect, no need to download content.\n\nLet me also consider: What if the redirect leads to another redirect? S3 pre-signed URLs don\'t redirect, they return 200 directly. So one level of redirect resolution should be enough for most cases.\n\nFor Actions artifact `archive_download_url`:\n- GET with Authorization → 302 to S3 URL\n\nFor release asset `browser_download_url` (via github.com):\n- GET with Authorization → 302 to objects.githubusercontent.com URL\n\nFor tarball/zipball:\n- GET with Authorization → 302 to CDN URL\n\nOne level of redirect should be sufficient for all these cases.\n\nHowever, there\'s another issue: **HTTPS and certificates**. `HttpURLConnection` handles HTTPS by default using the system certificate store, which should be fine on Android 7+.\n\nOK, here\'s my revised plan:\n\nIn `startAuthenticatedDownload`, or better in `checkStoragePermissionAndDownload`, before calling `startAuthenticatedDownload`:\n\n1. If URL is a GitHub API URL or github.com URL (likely to redirect):\n   - Launch a background thread\n   - Resolve the redirect URL (with auth)\n   - Call `startAuthenticatedDownload` with the final URL (WITHOUT auth)\n2. If URL is already a CDN/S3 URL:\n   - Call `startAuthenticatedDownload` directly (without auth)\n\nOR even simpler: ALWAYS try to resolve redirects first, then download the final URL without auth. If it\'s already a final URL (200 response), download it with auth.\n\nActually the simplest robust fix: Always resolve redirect → if redirected, download final URL without auth; if not redirected (200), download original URL with auth.\n\nLet me implement this. I\'ll add a Kotlin coroutine or Thread for the redirect resolution.\n\nAlso, I should make the Authorization header prefix consistent. The web code uses `Bearer`, our Android code uses `token`. Both should work for classic PAT tokens, but only `Bearer` works for fine-grained PAT. Let me use `Bearer` in the Android code too to match the web code.\n\nActually, looking at GitHub docs:\n- Classic PAT: Both `token <PAT>` and `Bearer <PAT>` work\n- Fine-grained PAT: Only `Bearer <PAT>` works\n- OAuth tokens: `Bearer <TOKEN>` works\n- GitHub Apps: `Bearer <JWT>` works\n\nSo using `Bearer` is more universal. Let me update the header.\n\nHere\'s the complete fix plan:\n\n**MainActivity.kt changes:**\n\n1. Add `resolveRedirectUrl()` function that uses `HttpURLConnection` to follow one level of redirect\n2. Modify `checkStoragePermissionAndDownload` / add new function `prepareAndDownload()` that:\n   - Runs on background thread\n   - Calls `resolveRedirectUrl(url, token)` to get final URL\n   - If redirected: `startAuthenticatedDownload(finalUrl, fileName, userAgent, "")` (no auth for pre-signed URL)\n   - If not redirected: `startAuthenticatedDownload(url, fileName, userAgent, token)` (keep auth for direct URLs)\n3. The issue is SPECIFICALLY that GitHub redirects to S3/CDN pre-signed URLs, and when DownloadManager follows the redirect, it sends the Authorization header to the S3 endpoint, which causes S3 to reject it.\n\nWait, actually does DownloadManager send the custom headers to redirect locations? Let me check...\n\nFrom Android documentation and various sources: `DownloadManager` does NOT strip custom headers when following redirects. So if you set `Authorization: token xxx` and GitHub redirects to S3, DownloadManager will send `Authorization: token xxx` to S3, which S3 will reject.\n\nHowever, I\'ve also seen conflicting reports. Some say DownloadManager strips custom headers on redirects, some say it doesn\'t. The behavior might vary by Android version.\n\nBut the bottom line: the user is experiencing download failures. The DownloadManager notification appears (so the request is being made) but the download fails (so something is wrong with the request).\n\nThe most likely cause is the Authorization header on redirected URLs. Let me fix it.\n\nHere\'s my revised approach - resolve the redirect first:\n\n```kotlin\n/** 在后台线程解析 GitHub 下载链接的最终 URL（跟随一级重定向） */\nprivate fun resolveDownloadUrl(\n    originalUrl: String,\n    token: String,\n    onResolved: (finalUrl: String, needsAuth: Boolean) -> Unit,\n) {\n    Thread {\n        runCatching {\n            val conn = (java.net.URL(originalUrl).openConnection() as java.net.HttpURLConnection).apply {\n                if (token.isNotBlank()) setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")\n                setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")\n                setRequestProperty("Accept", "application/octet-stream")\n                instanceFollowRedirects = false  // 手动处理重定向\n                requestMethod = "GET"\n                connectTimeout = 15_000\n                readTimeout = 5_000\n                // 不读响应体，拿到 Location 后立即断开\n            }\n            conn.connect()\n            val code = conn.responseCode\n            val location = conn.getHeaderField("Location")\n            conn.disconnect()\n\n            if (code in 300..399 && !location.isNullOrBlank()) {\n                // GitHub → 重定向到 S3/CDN 预签名 URL，不需要 Authorization\n                runOnUiThread { onResolved(location, false) }\n            } else {\n                // 直接可下载，携带认证\n                runOnUiThread { onResolved(originalUrl, token.isNotBlank()) }\n            }\n        }.onFailure {\n            // 解析失败则直接尝试（最坏情况 DownloadManager 自行处理）\n            runOnUiThread { onResolved(originalUrl, token.isNotBlank()) }\n        }\n    }.start()\n}\n```\n\nThen in `startAuthenticatedDownload`, call this first:\n\nActually, let me restructure. The flow becomes:\n\n`checkStoragePermissionAndDownload` → (permission check passes) → `resolveDownloadUrl` → callback: `startAuthenticatedDownload(finalUrl, fileName, userAgent, if(needsAuth) token else "")`\n\nThis is clean. Let me also update the WebAppBridge.downloadFile to use this flow.\n\nFor `saveBlobData` (ExportPage), since the data is already in memory and we\'re writing it directly, that doesn\'t go through DownloadManager, so it\'s not affected by this issue.\n\nLet me now write the final MainActivity.kt.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

THOUGHT: 问题根因确认：所有 GitHub 下载 URL（`browser_download_url`、`zipball_url`、`archive_download_url`）都会 **302 重定向**到 S3/CDN 预签名 URL。`DownloadManager` 跟随重定向时会把 `Authorization` header 也带过去，S3 预签名 URL 本身已含鉴权参数，额外的 `Authorization` header 直接导致 S3 返回 403 签名冲突，下载失败。系统通知出现是因为 `DownloadManager` 已入队，但下载本身报错。

**修复方案**：在提交给 `DownloadManager` 之前，先用 `HttpURLConnection`（禁止自动重定向）手动发一次请求，拿到 Location 后立即断开，再把最终预签名 URL 交给 `DownloadManager`（不带 auth header）。

package com.github.manager

import android.Manifest
import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.app.DownloadManager
import android.content.BroadcastReceiver
import android.content.ContentValues
import android.content.Context
import android.content.Intent
import android.content.IntentFilter
import android.content.pm.PackageManager
import android.graphics.Color
import android.net.Uri
import android.os.Build
import android.os.Bundle
import android.os.Environment
import android.os.Handler
import android.os.Looper
import android.provider.MediaStore
import android.util.Base64
import android.view.View
import android.webkit.JavascriptInterface
import android.webkit.URLUtil
import android.webkit.ValueCallback
import android.webkit.WebChromeClient
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.activity.result.contract.ActivityResultContracts
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.content.FileProvider
import java.io.File
import java.io.IOException
import java.net.HttpURLConnection
import java.net.URL

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View
    private var splashDismissed = false

    // ── 文件上传 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    private var fileChooserCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>? = null
    private var cameraImageUri: Uri? = null

    private val fileChooserLauncher = registerForActivityResult(
        ActivityResultContracts.StartActivityForResult()
    ) { result ->
        val uris: Array<Uri>? = if (result.resultCode == RESULT_OK) {
            result.data?.let { data ->
                when {
                    data.clipData != null ->
                        Array(data.clipData!!.itemCount) { i ->
                            data.clipData!!.getItemAt(i).uri
                        }
                    data.data != null -> arrayOf(data.data!!)
                    else -> cameraImageUri?.let { arrayOf(it) }
                }
            }
        } else null
        fileChooserCallback?.onReceiveValue(uris)
        fileChooserCallback = null
    }

    // ── 按需权限：相机 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    private var pendingFileChooserParams: WebChromeClient.FileChooserParams? = null
    private var pendingFilePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>? = null

    private val cameraPermissionLauncher = registerForActivityResult(
        ActivityResultContracts.RequestPermission()
    ) { granted ->
        val params = pendingFileChooserParams
        val callback = pendingFilePathCallback
        pendingFileChooserParams = null
        pendingFilePathCallback = null
        if (params != null && callback != null) {
            if (granted) launchFileChooser(params, callback)
            else launchFileChooserWithoutCamera(params, callback)
        }
    }

    // ── 按需权限：写存储（仅 API 26–28） ───────────────────────────
    private var pendingDownloadUrl: String = ""
    private var pendingDownloadFileName: String = ""
    private var pendingDownloadToken: String = ""

    private val writeStoragePermissionLauncher = registerForActivityResult(
        ActivityResultContracts.RequestPermission()
    ) { granted ->
        if (granted) {
            resolveAndDownload(pendingDownloadUrl, pendingDownloadFileName, pendingDownloadToken)
        } else {
            Toast.makeText(this, "存储权限被拒绝，无法保存文件", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        }
        pendingDownloadUrl = ""; pendingDownloadFileName = ""; pendingDownloadToken = ""
    }

    // ── 下载完成广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    private val downloadReceiver = object : BroadcastReceiver() {
        override fun onReceive(context: Context?, intent: Intent?) {
            Toast.makeText(context, "✓ 文件已下载完成，保存至「下载」文件夹", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    // ── JS 桥接口 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    inner class WebAppBridge {

        /** React 首屏就绪后调用，触发启动遮罩淡出 */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
        }

        /**
         * ArtifactsPage 调用：传原始 GitHub URL + token，由原生完成"解析重定向 → 下载"流程。
         *
         * GitHub 所有下载链接（releases/archive/artifacts）均会 302 重定向到
         * S3/CDN 预签名 URL。直接把 Authorization header 转发给预签名 URL 会
         * 触发 S3 签名冲突，导致下载失败。此方法先解析最终 URL 再下载，避免此问题。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.downloadFile(url, fileName, token)
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun downloadFile(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
            runOnUiThread {
                checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
            }
        }

        /**
         * ExportPage 调用：传内存文本内容（Base64 编码），由原生写入「下载」文件夹。
         * 适用于 JSON/CSV 导出等纯文本内容，不经过 DownloadManager。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData(fileName, mimeType, base64Content)
         * 此方法运行在 JavascriptInterface 后台线程。
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun saveBlobData(fileName: String, mimeType: String, base64Content: String) {
            if (base64Content.isEmpty()) {
                runOnUiThread {
                    Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "保存失败：内容为空", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                }
                return
            }
            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT < Build.VERSION_CODES.Q) {
                val granted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE) ==
                    PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED
                if (!granted) {
                    runOnUiThread {
                        Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "请授予存储权限后重试", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                    }
                    return
                }
            }
            runCatching {
                val bytes = Base64.decode(base64Content, Base64.DEFAULT)
                val savedName = if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.Q) {
                    saveToMediaStore(bytes, fileName, mimeType)
                } else {
                    saveToLegacyStorage(bytes, fileName)
                }
                runOnUiThread {
                    Toast.makeText(
                        this@MainActivity,
                        "✓ 已保存至「下载」文件夹：$savedName",
                        Toast.LENGTH_SHORT
                    ).show()
                }
            }.onFailure { e ->
                runOnUiThread {
                    Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "保存失败：${e.message}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // ── MediaStore / Legacy 存储写入 ────────────────────────────────

    private fun saveToMediaStore(bytes: ByteArray, fileName: String, mimeType: String): String {
        val effectiveMime = mimeType.ifBlank { "application/octet-stream" }.substringBefore(";")
        val cv = ContentValues().apply {
            put(MediaStore.Downloads.DISPLAY_NAME, fileName)
            put(MediaStore.Downloads.MIME_TYPE, effectiveMime)
            put(MediaStore.Downloads.IS_PENDING, 1)
        }
        val resolver = contentResolver
        val uri = resolver.insert(MediaStore.Downloads.EXTERNAL_CONTENT_URI, cv)
            ?: throw IOException("无法在 MediaStore 创建下载记录")
        resolver.openOutputStream(uri)?.use { it.write(bytes) }
        cv.clear()
        cv.put(MediaStore.Downloads.IS_PENDING, 0)
        resolver.update(uri, cv, null, null)
        return fileName
    }

    private fun saveToLegacyStorage(bytes: ByteArray, fileName: String): String {
        val dir = Environment.getExternalStoragePublicDirectory(Environment.DIRECTORY_DOWNLOADS)
        dir.mkdirs()
        var target = File(dir, fileName)
        val base = fileName.substringBeforeLast(".")
        val ext = fileName.substringAfterLast(".", "")
        var n = 1
        while (target.exists()) {
            target = File(dir, if (ext.isNotEmpty()) "$base($n).$ext" else "$base($n)")
            n++
        }
        target.writeBytes(bytes)
        return target.name
    }

    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        splashOverlay.animate().alpha(0f).setDuration(250)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }.start()
    }

    // ── 生命周期 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        window.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)

        registerDownloadReceiver()
        setupWebViewSettings()
        setupWebViewClient()
        setupWebChromeClient()
        setupDownloadListener()

        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)

        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        super.onDestroy()
        unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)
        webView.stopLoading()
        webView.destroy()
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }

    // ── WebView 配置 ────────────────────────────────────────────────

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    private fun setupWebViewSettings() {
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true
            allowContentAccess = true
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }
    }

    private fun setupWebViewClient() {
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                return !url.startsWith("file://") &&
                    !url.startsWith("https://") &&
                    !url.startsWith("http://")
            }
        }
    }

    private fun setupWebChromeClient() {
        webView.webChromeClient = object : WebChromeClient() {
            override fun onShowFileChooser(
                webView: WebView?,
                filePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>,
                fileChooserParams: FileChooserParams,
            ): Boolean {
                fileChooserCallback?.onReceiveValue(null)
                fileChooserCallback = filePathCallback

                val acceptTypes = fileChooserParams.acceptTypes?.toList() ?: emptyList()
                val needsCamera = acceptTypes.any { it.contains("image") || it.isEmpty() }
                val cameraGranted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.CAMERA) ==
                    PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED

                return when {
                    needsCamera && !cameraGranted -> {
                        pendingFileChooserParams = fileChooserParams
                        pendingFilePathCallback = filePathCallback
                        fileChooserCallback = null
                        cameraPermissionLauncher.launch(Manifest.permission.CAMERA)
                        true
                    }
                    else -> launchFileChooser(fileChooserParams, filePathCallback)
                }
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * DownloadListener：拦截 WebView 触发的下载。
     *
     * 两种场景：
     * 1. blob: URL（安全网）——前端通常已通过 AndroidBridge 处理，此处作为兜底。
     * 2. https: URL——从 localStorage 读取 token，走"解析重定向 → DownloadManager"流程。
     */
    private fun setupDownloadListener() {
        webView.setDownloadListener { url, _, contentDisposition, mimetype, _ ->
            val fileName = URLUtil.guessFileName(url, contentDisposition, mimetype)

            if (url.startsWith("blob:")) {
                // blob: URL 安全网：通过 JS 读内容再传给 saveBlobData
                val safeUrl = url.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
                val safeName = fileName.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
                val safeMime = mimetype.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
                val js = """
                    (function(){
                        fetch('$safeUrl')
                            .then(function(r){return r.blob();})
                            .then(function(blob){
                                var reader=new FileReader();
                                reader.onloadend=function(){
                                    var b64=(reader.result||'').toString().split(',')[1]||'';
                                    window.AndroidBridge&&window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData('$safeName','$safeMime',b64);
                                };
                                reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                            })
                            .catch(function(e){
                                console.warn('[AndroidDownload] blob fetch failed:',e.message);
                                window.AndroidBridge&&window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData('$safeName','','');
                            });
                    })()
                """.trimIndent()
                webView.evaluateJavascript(js, null)
                return@setDownloadListener
            }

            // https: URL：读取 token 后解析重定向再下载
            webView.evaluateJavascript(
                "(function(){ try { return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_token') || '' } catch(e){ return '' } })()"
            ) { result ->
                val token = result?.removeSurrounding("\"")?.trim() ?: ""
                checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
            }
        }
    }

    // ── 下载流程 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT <= Build.VERSION_CODES.P) {
            val granted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE) ==
                PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED
            if (!granted) {
                pendingDownloadUrl = url
                pendingDownloadFileName = fileName
                pendingDownloadToken = token
                writeStoragePermissionLauncher.launch(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE)
                return
            }
        }
        resolveAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
    }

    /**
     * 核心修复：先在后台线程解析 GitHub 下载链接的最终 URL，再交给 DownloadManager。
     *
     * 问题根因：
     *   GitHub 所有下载端点（browser_download_url / zipball / tarball / archive_download_url）
     *   均会返回 302 重定向到 AWS S3 或 CDN 的预签名 URL。
     *   DownloadManager 默认跟随重定向并转发所有自定义请求头，
     *   将 Authorization header 发送给 S3 预签名 URL 会触发签名冲突（403 SignatureDoesNotMatch），
     *   下载任务立刻失败——这就是"有通知但下载失败"的原因。
     *
     * 修复逻辑：
     *   1. 用 HttpURLConnection（禁止自动重定向）向原始 URL 发一次带 auth 的请求
     *   2. 若收到 3xx：取出 Location 头，用该预签名 URL 给 DownloadManager（不带 auth）
     *   3. 若收到 200（无重定向）：直接下载，携带 auth
     *   4. 若发生异常：回退到原始 URL + auth（降级处理）
     */
    private fun resolveAndDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
        Toast.makeText(this, "准备下载：$fileName", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()

        Thread {
            runCatching {
                val conn = (URL(url).openConnection() as HttpURLConnection).apply {
                    if (token.isNotBlank()) setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
                    setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")
                    setRequestProperty("Accept", "application/octet-stream")
                    instanceFollowRedirects = false   // 手动处理重定向，避免 auth 头泄露给 S3
                    requestMethod = "GET"
                    connectTimeout = 15_000
                    readTimeout = 5_000
                }
                conn.connect()
                val code = conn.responseCode
                val location = conn.getHeaderField("Location")
                conn.disconnect()

                when {
                    code in 300..399 && !location.isNullOrBlank() -> {
                        // GitHub → 重定向到预签名 URL，不携带 auth（预签名 URL 已含鉴权参数）
                        runOnUiThread { enqueueDownload(location, fileName, token = "") }
                    }
                    code == 200 -> {
                        // 直链，无重定向，携带 auth
                        runOnUiThread { enqueueDownload(url, fileName, token) }
                    }
                    else -> {
                        runOnUiThread {
                            Toast.makeText(
                                this, "下载准备失败（HTTP $code）", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT
                            ).show()
                        }
                    }
                }
            }.onFailure {
                // 网络异常等：直接尝试（DownloadManager 自行处理）
                runOnUiThread { enqueueDownload(url, fileName, token) }
            }
        }.start()
    }

    /** 将最终 URL 提交给 DownloadManager，token 为空时不发送 Authorization header */
    private fun enqueueDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
        runCatching {
            val request = DownloadManager.Request(Uri.parse(url)).apply {
                if (token.isNotBlank()) {
                    addRequestHeader("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
                }
                addRequestHeader("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")
                setTitle(fileName)
                setDescription("正在从 GitHub 下载：$fileName")
                setNotificationVisibility(
                    DownloadManager.Request.VISIBILITY_VISIBLE_NOTIFY_COMPLETED
                )
                setDestinationInExternalPublicDir(Environment.DIRECTORY_DOWNLOADS, fileName)
                setAllowedOverMetered(true)
                setAllowedOverRoaming(false)
            }
            val dm = getSystemService(DOWNLOAD_SERVICE) as DownloadManager
            dm.enqueue(request)
        }.onFailure { e ->
            Toast.makeText(this, "下载失败：${e.message}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    // ── 文件选择辅助 ────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun launchFileChooser(
        fileChooserParams: WebChromeClient.FileChooserParams,
        filePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>,
    ): Boolean {
        fileChooserCallback = filePathCallback
        val fileIntent = runCatching { fileChooserParams.createIntent() }.getOrNull()
            ?: Intent(Intent.ACTION_GET_CONTENT).apply {
                type = "*/*"; addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_OPENABLE)
                putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_ALLOW_MULTIPLE, true)
            }
        val cameraIntent = createCameraIntent()
        val chooserIntent = Intent.createChooser(fileIntent, "选择文件或拍照").apply {
            val extras = listOfNotNull(cameraIntent).toTypedArray()
            if (extras.isNotEmpty()) putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_INITIAL_INTENTS, extras)
        }
        return runCatching { fileChooserLauncher.launch(chooserIntent); true }
            .getOrElse { fileChooserCallback = null; false }
    }

    private fun launchFileChooserWithoutCamera(
        fileChooserParams: WebChromeClient.FileChooserParams,
        filePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>,
    ): Boolean {
        fileChooserCallback = filePathCallback
        val fileIntent = runCatching { fileChooserParams.createIntent() }.getOrNull()
            ?: Intent(Intent.ACTION_GET_CONTENT).apply {
                type = "*/*"; addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_OPENABLE)
                putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_ALLOW_MULTIPLE, true)
            }
        return runCatching {
            fileChooserLauncher.launch(Intent.createChooser(fileIntent, "选择文件"))
            true
        }.getOrElse { fileChooserCallback = null; false }
    }

    private fun createCameraIntent(): Intent? = runCatching {
        val imageFile = File.createTempFile("camera_capture_", ".jpg", externalCacheDir)
        val uri = FileProvider.getUriForFile(this, "$packageName.fileprovider", imageFile)
        cameraImageUri = uri
        Intent(android.provider.MediaStore.ACTION_IMAGE_CAPTURE).apply {
            putExtra(android.provider.MediaStore.EXTRA_OUTPUT, uri)
        }
    }.getOrNull()

    // ── 广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun registerDownloadReceiver() {
        val filter = IntentFilter(DownloadManager.ACTION_DOWNLOAD_COMPLETE)
        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.TIRAMISU) {
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter, Context.RECEIVER_NOT_EXPORTED)
        } else {
            @Suppress("UnspecifiedRegisterReceiverFlag")
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter)
        }
    }
}

Let me think about what could go wrong:\n\n1. We set `requestMethod = "GET"` with `instanceFollowRedirects = false`\n2. We call `conn.connect()`\n3. We read `conn.responseCode` - this sends the request and reads the response headers\n4. We read `conn.getHeaderField("Location")`\n\nThis should work. But what if the API returns 415?\n\nThe `Accept: application/octet-stream` header in the INITIAL request to GitHub API might be causing 415!\n\nHere\'s what I think is happening:\n- GitHub API at `api.github.com` for artifact downloads requires `Accept: application/vnd.github+json` OR at minimum doesn\'t reject other values\n- But sending `Accept: application/octet-stream` to `api.github.com` causes 415\n\nActually more likely: GitHub API requires a specific `Accept` header and rejects `application/octet-stream` with 415. This is unusual but possible.\n\nOr: The issue is that the INITIAL redirect resolution request itself is failing with 415 before we even get to DownloadManager.\n\nLet me check what headers we set:\n```kotlin\nsetRequestProperty("Accept", "application/octet-stream")\n```\n\nFor GitHub API endpoints, the Accept header should be `application/vnd.github+json` or wildcarded.\n\n**Fix**: Remove the `Accept: application/octet-stream` header from the initial redirect resolution request. Just use:\n- `Authorization: Bearer $token`  \n- `User-Agent: GitHub Manager Android`\n\nOr set Accept to `*/*` to be safe.\n\nAlso, let me reconsider: when we pass the URL to `enqueueDownload()` (which calls DownloadManager), the DownloadManager also doesn\'t add an Accept header by default, which is fine.\n\nThe `Accept: application/octet-stream` I added was thinking it would help with binary downloads, but for the GitHub API endpoints, it\'s actually causing issues.\n\n**Root cause**: The `Accept: application/octet-stream` header in `resolveAndDownload()` is causing GitHub API to return 415 Unsupported Media Type.\n\n**Fix**: Remove the Accept header from `resolveAndDownload()`, or set it to `*/*`.\n\nActually, thinking more about what `Accept: application/octet-stream` means:\n- We\'re asking the server to ONLY return `application/octet-stream` \n- GitHub API endpoints for artifacts/releases return JSON responses OR 302 redirects\n- GitHub API might see `Accept: application/octet-stream` and think "I can\'t provide this content type" → 415\n\nFor the redirect resolution step, we don\'t need `Accept` at all - we just need the 302 Location header. Thought: HTTP 415 = "Unsupported Media Type"，直接定位到问题：我们在 `resolveAndDownload()` 里发送了 `Accept: application/octet-stream` 给 GitHub API 端点。GitHub API（`api.github.com`）不接受 `application/octet-stream` 作为 Accept 类型，直接返回 415 拒绝请求，重定向解析根本没机会执行。

只需移除这个错误的 `Accept` 头——重定向解析阶段我们只需要 Location header，不需要指定内容类型。
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```

                    if (token.isNotBlank()) setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
                    setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")
                    setRequestProperty("Accept", "application/octet-stream")
                    instanceFollowRedirects = false   // 手动处理重定向，避免 auth 头泄露给 S3
                    requestMethod = "GET"
                    connectTimeout = 15_000
                    readTimeout = 5_000

```
New String: ```
                val conn = (URL(url).openConnection() as HttpURLConnection).apply {
                    if (token.isNotBlank()) setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
                    setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")
                    // ⚠️ 不设置 Accept 头：
                    //   GitHub API 端点（api.github.com）仅接受 application/vnd.github+json，
                    //   发送 application/octet-stream 会触发 415 Unsupported Media Type。

                    instanceFollowRedirects = false   // 手动处理重定向，避免 auth 头泄露给 S3
                    requestMethod = "GET"
                    connectTimeout = 15_000
                    readTimeout = 5_000
```

<action>
AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe issue: `type={showToken ? \'text\' : \'password\'}` - when `showToken` is false (default), the input is `type="password"`, which triggers the secure/safe keyboard on Android (a special keyboard that hides input and may limit copy-paste). \n\nThe user wants to NOT use the secure keyboard when inputting a GitHub token. The token is like `ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx` and needs to be pasted, so the secure keyboard restrictions are annoying.\n\nThe fix: Change the input to always use `type="text"` with `inputMode="none"` or better yet, just keep it as `type="text"` always, and use CSS to mask the characters when `showToken` is false.\n\nBut wait - how do we mask the text if we use `type="text"`? We can use CSS: `fontFamily: \'text-security-disc\'` or the `-webkit-text-security: disc` CSS property.\n\nActually, the simplest approach:\n1. Change `type` to always be `"text"` \n2. When not showing (hidden state), use CSS `-webkit-text-security: disc` to visually mask the input\n\nThis way:\n- The browser/WebView uses the normal text keyboard (not the secure keyboard)\n- The visual appearance still shows dots when `showToken` is false\n- The user can use normal copy-paste\n\nBut `-webkit-text-security` is a non-standard CSS property. Let me think of alternatives.\n\nAlternative: Use `type="text"` always, and when hidden, set `letter-spacing: 0.25em` and `font-size: 2em` to make it look like dots... nah that\'s too hacky.\n\nAnother approach: Keep `type="password"` for web browsers (where it\'s fine), but detect Android WebView and use `type="text"` with `autoComplete="new-password"` to prevent the secure keyboard.\n\nActually, the cleanest solution for Android WebView is:\n- `type="text"` always\n- `inputMode="text"` to explicitly request the text keyboard\n- Use CSS to visually mask: `-webkit-text-security: disc` when not showing\n\nWait, but `-webkit-text-security` is supported in WebKit/Chrome. Let me check:\n- Android WebView uses Chrome\'s Blink engine, so `-webkit-text-security` should work!\n\nSo the approach:\n1. Always use `type="text"`\n2. When `showToken` is false, add inline style `{ WebkitTextSecurity: \'disc\' }` (React style property)\n3. When `showToken` is true, `{ WebkitTextSecurity: \'none\' }`\n\nThis gives us:\n- Normal text keyboard (no secure keyboard)\n- Visual masking via CSS\n\nBut actually, wait. The issue might be more fundamental. On Android, when an input has `type="password"`, the Android system automatically shows the secure keyboard (PIN/password layout) which:\n1. Is harder to use for long token strings like `ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx`\n2. Restricts certain characters or input methods\n3. Doesn\'t allow clipboard paste on some devices\n\nBy changing to `type="text"`, we get the normal QWERTY keyboard which is much better for typing a GitHub token.\n\nLet me implement the clean fix:\n- `type="text"` always (no more `type="password"`)\n- Add `inputMode="none"` ... no, that disables the keyboard entirely\n- Add `autoComplete="off"` (already there)\n- Use CSS `-webkit-text-security: disc` for masking when `showToken` is false\n\nThis is the best approach. Let me write it.\n\nIn React, CSS properties with vendor prefixes are written in camelCase: `WebkitTextSecurity`.\n\n```tsx\n<Input\n  id="token"\n  type="text"   // Always text, never password - prevents secure keyboard on Android\n  inputMode="text"\n  value={token}\n  onChange={(e) => setToken(e.target.value)}\n  placeholder="ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"\n  className="pl-10 pr-10 bg-secondary border-border text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus:border-primary focus:ring-primary font-mono text-sm"\n  style={showToken ? undefined : { WebkitTextSecurity: \'disc\' } as React.CSSProperties}\n  autoComplete="off"\n  autoCorrect="off"\n  autoCapitalize="off"\n  spellCheck={false}\n/>\n```\n\nThis is a minimal, clean change that solves the problem perfectly.\n\nAlso adding `autoCorrect="off"` and `autoCapitalize="off"` which are good for token inputs on mobile.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

    82 function RepoContextMenu({ repo, onDeleteSuccess }: { repo: GitHubRepo; onDeleteSuccess: () => void }) {
    83   const navigate = useNavigate();
    84   const [deleteDialogOpen, setDeleteDialogOpen] = useState(false);
    85   const [confirmName, setConfirmName] = useState('');
    86   const [deleting, setDeleting] = useState(false);
    87 
    88   const handleStar = async () => {
    89     try {
    90       await starRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
    91       toast.success(`已为 ${repo.name} 加星`);
    92     } catch {
    93       toast.error('操作失败');
    94     }
    95   };
    96 
    97   const handleUnstar = async () => {
    98     try {
    99       await unstarRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
   100       toast.success(`已取消 ${repo.name} 的星标`);
   101     } catch {
   102       toast.error('操作失败');
   103     }
   104   };
   105 
   106   const handleFork = async () => {
   107     try {
   108       toast.info('正在 Fork 仓库...');
   109       await forkRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
   110       toast.success(`Fork 成功！`);
   111     } catch {
   112       toast.error('Fork 失败');
   113     }
   114   };
   115 
   116   const handleCopyUrl = () => {
   117     navigator.clipboard.writeText(repo.clone_url || repo.html_url);
   118     toast.success('仓库地址已复制');
   119   };
   120 
   121   const handleDelete = async () => {
   122     if (confirmName !== repo.name) { toast.error('仓库名称不一致'); return; }
   123     setDeleting(true);
   124     try {
   125       await deleteRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
   126       toast.success(`已删除仓库 ${repo.name}`);
   127       setDeleteDialogOpen(false);
   128       // 通知父组件刷新列表，避免 window.location.reload() 导致 GitHub Pages 空白页
   129       onDeleteSuccess();
   130     } catch {
   131       toast.error('删除失败，请确认你有足够权限');
   132     } finally {
   133       setDeleting(false);
   134     }
   135   };
   136 
   137   return (
   138     <>
   139       <ContextMenuContent className="bg-popover border-border w-52">
   140         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm"
   141           onClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${repo.full_name}`)}>
   142           <BookOpen className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />查看仓库详情
   143         </ContextMenuItem>
   144         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm"
   145           onClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${repo.full_name}/code`)}>
   146           <Code2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />浏览代码
   147         </ContextMenuItem>
   148         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm"
   149           onClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${repo.full_name}/commits/${repo.default_branch}`)}>
   150           <GitBranch className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />查看提交记录
   151         </ContextMenuItem>
   152         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm"
   153           onClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${repo.full_name}/pulls`)}>
   154           <GitPullRequest className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />查看 Pull Requests
   155         </ContextMenuItem>
   156         <ContextMenuSeparator className="bg-border" />
   157         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm" onClick={handleStar}>
   158           <Star className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />Star 仓库
   159         </ContextMenuItem>
   160         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm" onClick={handleUnstar}>
   161           <Star className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2 fill-current" />取消 Star
   162         </ContextMenuItem>
   163         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm" onClick={handleFork}>
   164           <GitFork className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />Fork 仓库
   165         </ContextMenuItem>
   166         <ContextMenuSeparator className="bg-border" />
   167         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm" onClick={handleCopyUrl}>
   168           <Copy className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />复制仓库地址
   169         </ContextMenuItem>
   170         <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm" asChild>
   171           <a href={repo.html_url} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
   172             <ExternalLink className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />在 GitHub 中打开
   173           </a>
   174         </ContextMenuItem>
   175         <ContextMenuSeparator className="bg-border" />
   176         <ContextMenuItem
   177           className="text-destructive cursor-pointer text-sm focus:text-destructive"
   178           onClick={() => { setConfirmName(''); setDeleteDialogOpen(true); }}
   179         >
   180           <Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2" />删除仓库
   181         </ContextMenuItem>
   182       </ContextMenuContent>
   183 
   184       {/* 删除确认对话框 */}
   185       <AlertDialog open={deleteDialogOpen} onOpenChange={setDeleteDialogOpen}>

function SearchRepoContextMenu({ repo, children }: { repo: GitHubRepo; children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const handleStar = async () => {
    try {
      await starRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
      toast.success(`已为 ${repo.name} 加星`);
    } catch { toast.error('操作失败'); }
  };

  const handleUnstar = async () => {
    try {
      await unstarRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
      toast.success(`已取消 ${repo.name} 的星标`);
    } catch { toast.error('操作失败'); }
  };

  const handleFork = async () => {
    try {
      toast.info('正在 Fork 仓库...');
      await forkRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
      toast.success('Fork 成功！');
    } catch { toast.error('Fork 失败'); }
  };

  const handleCopyUrl = () => {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(repo.clone_url || repo.html_url);
    toast.success('仓库地址已复制');
  };

  return (
    <ContextMenu>
      <ContextMenuTrigger asChild>{children}</ContextMenuTrigger>
      <ContextMenuContent className="bg-popover border-border w-52">
        <ContextMenuItem className="text-foreground cursor-pointer text-sm"
          onClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${repo.full_name}`)}>

  // 用 useMemo 稳定匹配结果，避免每次渲染产生新数组导致 useCallback 失效
  const fsSearchMatches = useMemo<Array<{ start: number; end: number }>>(() => {
    if (!editorFullscreen || !searchQuery.trim()) return [];
    const lower = editContent.toLowerCase();
    const q = searchQuery.toLowerCase();
    const matches: Array<{ start: number; end: number }> = [];
    let pos = 0;
    while (pos < lower.length) {
      const idx = lower.indexOf(q, pos);
      if (idx === -1) break;
      matches.push({ start: idx, end: idx + q.length });
      // 非重叠匹配：跳过整个关键词长度，防止重叠导致高亮节点越界串位
      pos = idx + q.length;
    }
    return matches;
  }, [editorFullscreen, searchQuery, editContent]);

  const fsMatchCount = fsSearchMatches.length;
  const fsSafeIndex = fsMatchCount > 0 ? ((searchMatchIndex % fsMatchCount) + fsMatchCount) % fsMatchCount : 0;

  const loadContents = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!owner || !repo || !currentBranch) return;
    setLoading(true);
    setFileContent(null);
    setFileBase64(null);
    setCurrentFile(null);
    // 加载新路径时重置编辑器状态
    setEditorFullscreen(false);
    setActionMode(null);
    setEditContent('');
    setCommitMsg('');
    setShowSearch(false);
    setSearchQuery('');
    setSearchMatchIndex(0);
    try {
      const data = await getRepoContents(owner, repo, filePath, currentBranch);
      if (Array.isArray(data)) {
        const sorted = [...data].sort((a, b) => {
          if (a.type === 'dir' && b.type !== 'dir') return -1;
          if (a.type !== 'dir' && b.type === 'dir') return 1;
          return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
        });
        setContents(sorted);
      } else {
        setCurrentFile(data);
        if (data.content && data.encoding === 'base64') {
          const raw = data.content.replace(/\n/g, '');
          setFileBase64(raw);
          if (!isImageFile(data.name)) {
            const decoded = decodeBase64Content(data.content);
            setFileContent(decoded);
            // 文本文件：直接在此原子性地打开编辑器，避免 useEffect 竞态
            setEditContent(decoded);
            setCommitMsg(`Update ${data.name}`);
            setActionMode('edit');
            setEditorFullscreen(true);
          }
        } else {
          setFileContent('（无法解码文件内容）');
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('加载文件内容失败');
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, [owner, repo, filePath, currentBranch]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!owner || !repo) return;
    getBranches(owner, repo)
      .then((result) => {
        setBranches(result.data);
        if (result.data.length > 0 && !currentBranch) {
          setCurrentBranch(result.data[0].name);
        }
      })
      .catch(console.error);
  }, [owner, repo, currentBranch]);

  useEffect(() => { loadContents(); }, [loadContents]);
[The command completed with exit code 0.]

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nNow I have a clear picture. Let me analyze ALL the issues:\n\n## Identified Issues\n\n### 1. CodeBrowserPage - "编辑文件" in FileContextMenuContent\n\n**Bug**: In the file list view (when displaying a directory), when you right-click on a file and select "编辑文件", it calls `openAction(\'edit\')` WITHOUT passing the item.\n\n```tsx\n<ContextMenuItem onClick={() => openAction(\'edit\')}>\n  <Pencil />编辑文件\n</ContextMenuItem>\n```\n\nIn `openAction`:\n```ts\nif (mode === \'edit\' && fileContent) {\n  // This branch requires fileContent to be set\n  // But when viewing a directory listing, fileContent = null\n  // So nothing happens - the editor never opens!\n```\n\n**Fix**: When "编辑文件" is clicked from the file list, we should navigate to the file page (which will automatically open the editor via `loadContents`). The navigate to the file path IS what triggers the edit mode (look at line 233-238 in loadContents - when it loads a file, it sets `setActionMode(\'edit\')` and `setEditorFullscreen(true)` automatically!\n\nSo the fix for "编辑文件" in FileContextMenuContent is simply:\n```tsx\nonClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${owner}/${repo}/code/${item.path}`)}\n// or keep it as navigating to the file (which auto-opens editor)\n```\n\nActually wait - looking at loadContents again at line 236-238:\n```ts\nsetActionMode(\'edit\');\nsetEditorFullscreen(true);\n```\n\nWait, but this opens the editor when ANY file is loaded, not just when editing. Let me re-read...\n\nActually looking at line 227-238:\n```\nsetCurrentFile(data);\nif (data.content && data.encoding === \'base64\') {\n  const raw = data.content.replace(/\\n/g, \'\');\n  setFileBase64(raw);\n  if (!isImageFile(data.name)) {\n    const decoded = decodeBase64Content(data.content);\n    setFileContent(decoded);\n    // 文本文件：直接在此原子性地打开编辑器，避免 useEffect 竞态\n    setEditContent(decoded);\n    setCommitMsg(`Update ${data.name}`);\n    setActionMode(\'edit\');\n    setEditorFullscreen(true);\n  }\n}\n```\n\nOh interesting - it seems like when a non-image file is loaded, it AUTOMATICALLY opens the editor in fullscreen! So navigating to the file IS the same as editing it.\n\nBut that means "查看文件" and "编辑文件" do the SAME THING when the file is a non-image text file. Both navigate to `item.path`.\n\nThe real fix for "编辑文件" from the file list: it should navigate to the file, which will auto-open the editor. The APIs work.\n\n### 3. NotificationsPage - No click-through to notification subject (UX issue)\nClicking a notification row doesn\'t navigate anywhere. The `notification.subject.url` is an API URL (like `https://api.github.com/repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}`), not a web URL. We need to parse this to route to the right page in the app.\n\nFor example:\n- `https://api.github.com/repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}` → navigate to `/repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}`\n- `https://api.github.com/repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{number}` → navigate to `/repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{number}`\n- Others: open `notification.repository.html_url` in GitHub\n\n**Fix**: Parse the API URL to determine the type and number, then navigate to the appropriate in-app route. function getEventTypeInfo(type: string): { label: string; color: string } {
  const types: Record<string, { label: string; color: string }> = {
    PushEvent: { label: '推送', color: 'bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/30' },
    CreateEvent: { label: '创建', color: 'bg-success/10 text-success border-success/30' },
    DeleteEvent: { label: '删除', color: 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive border-destructive/30' },
    IssuesEvent: { label: 'Issue', color: 'bg-warning/10 text-warning border-warning/30' },
    PullRequestEvent: { label: 'Pull Request', color: 'bg-chart-4/10 text-chart-4 border-chart-4/30' },
    WatchEvent: { label: '收藏', color: 'bg-warning/10 text-warning border-warning/30' },
    ForkEvent: { label: 'Fork', color: 'bg-accent/10 text-accent border-accent/30' },
    IssueCommentEvent: { label: '评论', color: 'bg-secondary text-muted-foreground border-border' },
    PullRequestReviewEvent: { label: '审查', color: 'bg-chart-3/10 text-chart-3 border-chart-3/30' },
    ReleaseEvent: { label: '发布', color: 'bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/30' },
    PublicEvent: { label: '开源', color: 'bg-success/10 text-success border-success/30' },
    MemberEvent: { label: '成员', color: 'bg-accent/10 text-accent border-accent/30' },
  };
  return types[type] || { label: type.replace('Event', ''), color: 'bg-secondary text-muted-foreground border-border' };
}

    28 export default function NotificationsPage() {

New String: ```
  const handleMarkRead = async (id: string) => {
    try {
      await markNotificationRead(id);
      setNotifications((prev) =>
        prev.map((n) => (n.id === id ? { ...n, unread: false } : n))
      );
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('标记失败');
      console.error(err);
    }
  };

  /** 解析 GitHub API URL 提取应用内路由，例如：
   *  https://api.github.com/repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}
   *  → /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}
   */
  const resolveNotificationRoute = (notification: GitHubNotification): string | null => {
    const repoFullName = notification.repository.full_name; // owner/repo
    const url = notification.subject.url || '';
    const type = notification.subject.type;

    // 尝试从 API URL 末尾提取 issue/PR 编号
    const numberMatch = url.match(/\/(\d+)$/);
    const number = numberMatch ? numberMatch[1] : null;

    switch (type) {
      case 'Issue':
        return number ? `/repos/${repoFullName}/issues/${number}` : `/repos/${repoFullName}/issues`;
      case 'PullRequest':
        return number ? `/repos/${repoFullName}/pulls/${number}` : `/repos/${repoFullName}/pulls`;
      case 'Release':
        return `/repos/${repoFullName}/artifacts`;
      case 'CheckSuite':
        return `/repos/${repoFullName}/actions`;
      case 'Commit':
        return `/repos/${repoFullName}/commits/${repoFullName.split('/')[1]}`;
      default:
        return `/repos/${repoFullName}`;
    }
  };

  /** 点击通知：自动标为已读并跳转到对应页面 */
  const handleNotificationClick = async (notification: GitHubNotification) => {
    if (notification.unread) {
      // 乐观更新 UI，再执行 API 调用
      setNotifications((prev) =>
        prev.map((n) => (n.id === notification.id ? { ...n, unread: false } : n))
      );
      markNotificationRead(notification.id).catch(() => {
        // 回滚
        setNotifications((prev) =>
          prev.map((n) => (n.id === notification.id ? { ...n, unread: true } : n))
        );
      });
    }
    const route = resolveNotificationRoute(notification);
    if (route) navigate(route);
  };
```

</action>

```
// 仓库右键上下文菜单
function RepoContextMenu({ repo, onDeleteSuccess }: { repo: GitHubRepo; onDeleteSuccess: () => void }) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [deleteDialogOpen, setDeleteDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  const [confirmName, setConfirmName] = useState('');
  const [deleting, setDeleting] = useState(false);

  const handleToggleStar = async () => {
    try {
      const starred = await checkStarred(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
      if (starred) {
        await unstarRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
        toast.success(`已取消 ${repo.name} 的 Star`);
      } else {
        await starRepo(repo.owner.login, repo.name);
        toast.success(`已为 ${repo.name} 加 Star ⭐`);
      }
    } catch {
      toast.error('操作失败');
    }
  };
```

New String: ```
export default function ActivityPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [events, setEvents] = useState<GitHubEvent[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [loadingMore, setLoadingMore] = useState(false);

  /** 根据事件类型计算应用内跳转路由 */
  const getEventRoute = (event: GitHubEvent): string => {
    const repoName = event.repo.name; // owner/repo 格式
    const payload = event.payload as Record<string, unknown>;
    switch (event.type) {
      case 'IssuesEvent': {
        const issue = payload.issue as { number?: number } | undefined;
        return issue?.number
          ? `/repos/${repoName}/issues/${issue.number}`
          : `/repos/${repoName}/issues`;
      }
      case 'PullRequestEvent': {
        const pr = payload.pull_request as { number?: number } | undefined;
        return pr?.number
          ? `/repos/${repoName}/pulls/${pr.number}`
          : `/repos/${repoName}/pulls`;
      }
      case 'IssueCommentEvent': {
        const issue = payload.issue as { number?: number } | undefined;
        return issue?.number
          ? `/repos/${repoName}/issues/${issue.number}`
          : `/repos/${repoName}/issues`;
      }
      case 'PullRequestReviewEvent': {
        const pr = payload.pull_request as { number?: number } | undefined;
        return pr?.number
          ? `/repos/${repoName}/pulls/${pr.number}`
          : `/repos/${repoName}/pulls`;
      }
      case 'PushEvent':
        return `/repos/${repoName}/commits/${repoName.split('/')[1]}`;
      case 'ReleaseEvent':
        return `/repos/${repoName}/artifacts`;
      case 'CreateEvent':
      case 'DeleteEvent':
      case 'WatchEvent':
      case 'ForkEvent':
      case 'PublicEvent':
      case 'MemberEvent':
      default:
        return `/repos/${repoName}`;
    }
  };
```

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/src/pages/CodeBrowserPage.tsx]
Thought: 根因清楚：`download_url` 是 `raw.githubusercontent.com` 直链，所有下载都用裸 `<a href>` 打开，私有仓库没有携带 `Authorization` 头所以返回 404/登录页；即使是公开仓库，在 Android WebView 里文本文件也只会"在线查看"而不触发下载。需要用和 ArtifactsPage 相同的带鉴权下载函数替换三处裸链接。
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
import {
  getRepoContents,
  getBranches,
  updateFileContent,
  createFileContent,
  deleteFileContent,
  getFileInfo,
  deleteFolderContents,
} from '@/services/github';
import type { GitHubContent, GitHubBranch } from '@/types/types';

```
New String: ```
import {
  getRepoContents,
  getBranches,
  updateFileContent,
  createFileContent,
  deleteFileContent,
  getFileInfo,
  deleteFolderContents,
} from '@/services/github';
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import type { GitHubContent, GitHubBranch } from '@/types/types';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { decodeBase64Content } from '@/lib/utils';
import { getFileIconInfo, isImageFile } from '@/components/common/FileIcon';

/**
 * 带认证下载文件（raw.githubusercontent.com 私有仓库需 Bearer token）。
 *
 * Android：检测到 AndroidBridge 时直接将 URL + token 交给原生 DownloadManager，
 *   避免 WebView 将 raw URL 拦截为"在线查看"而非下载。
 * 浏览器：fetch + Authorization header → Blob → <a download>，
 *   确保私有仓库文件正常下载且文件名正确。
 */
async function downloadCodeFile(url: string, filename: string, token: string): Promise<void> {
  const bridge = (window as unknown as {
    AndroidBridge?: { downloadFile?: (u: string, f: string, t: string) => void }
  }).AndroidBridge;
  if (bridge?.downloadFile) {
    bridge.downloadFile(url, filename, token);
    return;
  }
  const headers: Record<string, string> = {};
  if (token) headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;
  const res = await fetch(url, { headers });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
  const blob = await res.blob();
  const blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = blobUrl;
  a.download = filename;
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  document.body.removeChild(a);
  URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl);
}
```
